### edit - 2026-04-08 17:22:07 UTC [19:22:07 CEST] (Redirected)

**User Request:** the new "tour" feature seems to offer "randomly related (?) nodes" - I would have expected that you take me through the nodes which are presented as related - and before the user clicks on (tour), you could fade in/out the related nodes (in the sequence if the tour) as well as the tour button to invite the user to take a tour

**Tool:** edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "filePath": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/_work/rapid-automations/integrations/operational-knowledge-<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>sal.ts",
  "oldString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a recommended reading order for nodes starting from a selected entity.\n * Two strategies:\n *   1. Incident/operational: prioritise causal chains (CAUSED_BY, HAS_ROOT_CAUSE,\n *      HAS_SYMPTOM) then resolutions, then structural, then operational edges.\n *   2. Documentation/business: follow PART_OF/CONTAINS/DERIVED_FROM hierarchy.\n *\n * The output is an ordered list of entity keys the user should visit.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    // Documentation mode: structural edges first\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  // Incident / operational mode: causal chain first\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided reading sequence from a starting entity.\n *\n * Uses priority-weighted BFS: edges with lower priority tiers are explored\n * before higher ones.  Limits the sequence to `maxNodes` to avoid\n * overwhelming the user.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n * @param maxNodes  Maximum number of nodes in the sequence (default 12).\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n  maxNodes = 12,\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [] };\n\n  // Determine mode based on the starting entity's ontology class\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Build adjacency list: key -> sorted neighbor list\n  // Each neighbor entry: { key, edgeType, priority }\n  interface Neighbor { key: string; edgeType: string; priority: number }\n  const adjacency = new Map<string, Neighbor[]>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    const addNeighbor = (from: string, to: string) => {\n      if (!entityMap.has(to)) return;\n      const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n      if (!adjacency.has(from)) adjacency.set(from, []);\n      adjacency.get(from)!.push({ key: to, edgeType: edge.type, priority: prio });\n    };\n    addNeighbor(edge.source, edge.target);\n    addNeighbor(edge.target, edge.source);\n  }\n\n  // Sort each adjacency list by priority (stable — preserves insertion order for ties)\n  for (const [, neighbors] of adjacency) {\n    neighbors.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);\n  }\n\n  // Priority BFS — process neighbors in priority order\n  const visited = new Set<string>();\n  const result: string[] = [];\n\n  // Use a simple queue seeded with the start node\n  const queue: string[] = [startKey];\n  visited.add(startKey);\n\n  while (queue.length > 0 && result.length < maxNodes) {\n    const current = queue.shift()!;\n    result.push(current);\n\n    const neighbors = adjacency.get(current) || [];\n    for (const n of neighbors) {\n      if (!visited.has(n.key) && result.length + queue.length < maxNodes) {\n        visited.add(n.key);\n        queue.push(n.key);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const labels = result.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n\n  return { nodeKeys: result, labels };\n}",
  "newString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a tour through the **direct neighbors** of the selected entity —\n * exactly the nodes shown in the Relationships panel.  The sequence starts\n * with the seed node and then visits each direct neighbor ordered by edge-type\n * priority (causal first, correlation last).\n *\n * Two priority strategies based on the starting entity's ontology class:\n *   1. Incident/operational (default): causal > resolution > structural > operational > data-flow.\n *   2. Documentation/business: structural > resolution > causal > operational > data-flow.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n  /** The edge type connecting each neighbor to the seed (index 0 is empty for seed). */\n  edgeTypes: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided tour through the direct neighbors of a starting entity.\n *\n * The result is [seed, ...directNeighbors] where neighbors are sorted by\n * edge-type priority.  This matches exactly what the user sees in the\n * Relationships section of the detail panel — no multi-hop surprises.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [], edgeTypes: [] };\n\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Collect direct neighbors with their best (lowest) edge priority.\n  // A neighbor may be connected via multiple edge types — keep the\n  // highest-priority (lowest number) one for ordering, but deduplicate\n  // the neighbor itself.\n  const neighborBest = new Map<string, { priority: number; edgeType: string }>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    let neighborKey: string | null = null;\n    if (edge.source === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.target)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.target;\n    } else if (edge.target === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.source)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.source;\n    }\n    if (!neighborKey) continue;\n\n    const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n    const existing = neighborBest.get(neighborKey);\n    if (!existing || prio < existing.priority) {\n      neighborBest.set(neighborKey, { priority: prio, edgeType: edge.type });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Sort neighbors by priority (lower = visit first), then alphabetically by name for stability\n  const sorted = [...neighborBest.entries()].sort((a, b) => {\n    const prioDiff = a[1].priority - b[1].priority;\n    if (prioDiff !== 0) return prioDiff;\n    const nameA = entityMap.get(a[0])?.name ?? a[0];\n    const nameB = entityMap.get(b[0])?.name ?? b[0];\n    return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n  });\n\n  const nodeKeys = [startKey, ...sorted.map(([k]) => k)];\n  const labels = nodeKeys.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n  const edgeTypes = ['', ...sorted.map(([, v]) => v.edgeType)];\n\n  return { nodeKeys, labels, edgeTypes };\n}"
}

{
  "filePath": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/_work/rapid-automations/integrations/operational-knowledge-<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>sal.ts",
  "oldString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a recommended reading order for nodes starting from a selected entity.\n * Two strategies:\n *   1. Incident/operational: prioritise causal chains (CAUSED_BY, HAS_ROOT_CAUSE,\n *      HAS_SYMPTOM) then resolutions, then structural, then operational edges.\n *   2. Documentation/business: follow PART_OF/CONTAINS/DERIVED_FROM hierarchy.\n *\n * The output is an ordered list of entity keys the user should visit.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    // Documentation mode: structural edges first\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  // Incident / operational mode: causal chain first\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided reading sequence from a starting entity.\n *\n * Uses priority-weighted BFS: edges with lower priority tiers are explored\n * before higher ones.  Limits the sequence to `maxNodes` to avoid\n * overwhelming the user.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n * @param maxNodes  Maximum number of nodes in the sequence (default 12).\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n  maxNodes = 12,\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [] };\n\n  // Determine mode based on the starting entity's ontology class\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Build adjacency list: key -> sorted neighbor list\n  // Each neighbor entry: { key, edgeType, priority }\n  interface Neighbor { key: string; edgeType: string; priority: number }\n  const adjacency = new Map<string, Neighbor[]>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    const addNeighbor = (from: string, to: string) => {\n      if (!entityMap.has(to)) return;\n      const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n      if (!adjacency.has(from)) adjacency.set(from, []);\n      adjacency.get(from)!.push({ key: to, edgeType: edge.type, priority: prio });\n    };\n    addNeighbor(edge.source, edge.target);\n    addNeighbor(edge.target, edge.source);\n  }\n\n  // Sort each adjacency list by priority (stable — preserves insertion order for ties)\n  for (const [, neighbors] of adjacency) {\n    neighbors.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);\n  }\n\n  // Priority BFS — process neighbors in priority order\n  const visited = new Set<string>();\n  const result: string[] = [];\n\n  // Use a simple queue seeded with the start node\n  const queue: string[] = [startKey];\n  visited.add(startKey);\n\n  while (queue.length > 0 && result.length < maxNodes) {\n    const current = queue.shift()!;\n    result.push(current);\n\n    const neighbors = adjacency.get(current) || [];\n    for (const n of neighbors) {\n      if (!visited.has(n.key) && result.length + queue.length < maxNodes) {\n        visited.add(n.key);\n        queue.push(n.key);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const labels = result.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n\n  return { nodeKeys: result, labels };\n}",
  "newString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a tour through the **direct neighbors** of the selected entity —\n * exactly the nodes shown in the Relationships panel.  The sequence starts\n * with the seed node and then visits each direct neighbor ordered by edge-type\n * priority (causal first, correlation last).\n *\n * Two priority strategies based on the starting entity's ontology class:\n *   1. Incident/operational (default): causal > resolution > structural > operational > data-flow.\n *   2. Documentation/business: structural > resolution > causal > operational > data-flow.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n  /** The edge type connecting each neighbor to the seed (index 0 is empty for seed). */\n  edgeTypes: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided tour through the direct neighbors of a starting entity.\n *\n * The result is [seed, ...directNeighbors] where neighbors are sorted by\n * edge-type priority.  This matches exactly what the user sees in the\n * Relationships section of the detail panel — no multi-hop surprises.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [], edgeTypes: [] };\n\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Collect direct neighbors with their best (lowest) edge priority.\n  // A neighbor may be connected via multiple edge types — keep the\n  // highest-priority (lowest number) one for ordering, but deduplicate\n  // the neighbor itself.\n  const neighborBest = new Map<string, { priority: number; edgeType: string }>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    let neighborKey: string | null = null;\n    if (edge.source === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.target)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.target;\n    } else if (edge.target === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.source)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.source;\n    }\n    if (!neighborKey) continue;\n\n    const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n    const existing = neighborBest.get(neighborKey);\n    if (!existing || prio < existing.priority) {\n      neighborBest.set(neighborKey, { priority: prio, edgeType: edge.type });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Sort neighbors by priority (lower = visit first), then alphabetically by name for stability\n  const sorted = [...neighborBest.entries()].sort((a, b) => {\n    const prioDiff = a[1].priority - b[1].priority;\n    if (prioDiff !== 0) return prioDiff;\n    const nameA = entityMap.get(a[0])?.name ?? a[0];\n    const nameB = entityMap.get(b[0])?.name ?? b[0];\n    return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n  });\n\n  const nodeKeys = [startKey, ...sorted.map(([k]) => k)];\n  const labels = nodeKeys.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n  const edgeTypes = ['', ...sorted.map(([, v]) => v.edgeType)];\n\n  return { nodeKeys, labels, edgeTypes };\n}"
}
```

  "newString": "/**\n * Get the subset of upcoming node keys for visual hinting.\n * Returns the next N nodes after the current position (not including current).\n */\nexport function getUpcomingKeys(\n  sequence: Pick<GuidedSequence, 'nodeKeys'>,\n  currentIndex: number,\n  count = 3,\n): string[] {\n  if (sequence.nodeKeys.length === 0) return [];\n  const start = currentIndex + 1;\n  return sequence.nodeKeys.slice(start, start + count);\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute the set of direct neighbor keys for a given entity.\n * Used by the pre-tour preview animation to know which nodes to cycle through.\n */\nexport function getDirectNeighborKeys(\n  entityKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n): string[] {\n  const entitySet = new Set(entities.map((e) => e.key));\n  const neighbors = new Set<string>();\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    if (edge.source === entityKey && entitySet.has(edge.target)) {\n      neighbors.add(edge.target);\n    } else if (edge.target === entityKey && entitySet.has(edge.source)) {\n      neighbors.add(edge.source);\n    }\n  }\n  return [...neighbors];\n}"
}

### edit - 2026-04-08 17:22:07 UTC [19:22:07 CEST] (Redirected)

**User Request:** the new "tour" feature seems to offer "randomly related (?) nodes" - I would have expected that you take me through the nodes which are presented as related - and before the user clicks on (tour), you could fade in/out the related nodes (in the sequence if the tour) as well as the tour button to invite the user to take a tour

**Tool:** edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "filePath": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/_work/rapid-automations/integrations/operational-knowledge-<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>geGraph/NodeDetails.tsx",
  "newString": "  const handleStopTour = useCallback(() => {\n    dispatch(stopGuidedTour());\n  }, [dispatch]);\n\n  // --- Pre-tour preview: cycle through direct neighbors when node selected,\n  // tour not active, and there are neighbors to show.  Each neighbor is\n  // highlighted for 1.5s, then the next one.  This gives the user a subtle\n  // preview of what the Tour will cover and draws attention to the Tour button.\n  const previewIntervalRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null>(null);\n  const previewIndexRef = useRef(0);\n\n  const neighborKeys = useMemo(() => {\n    if (!selectedKey) return [];\n    return getDirectNeighborKeys(selectedKey, entities, edges);\n  }, [selectedKey, entities, edges]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // Clear any existing interval\n    if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n      clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n      previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n    }\n\n    // Only run preview when: node selected, tour NOT active, has neighbors\n    if (!selectedKey || guidedTourActive || neighborKeys.length === 0) {\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Start cycling after a short initial delay\n    previewIndexRef.current = 0;\n    dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[0]));\n\n    previewIntervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {\n      previewIndexRef.current = (previewIndexRef.current + 1) % neighborKeys.length;\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[previewIndexRef.current]));\n    }, 1500);\n\n    return () => {\n      if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n        clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n        previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n      }\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n    };\n  }, [selectedKey, guidedTourActive, neighborKeys, dispatch]);",
  "oldString": "  const handleStopTour = useCallback(() => {\n    dispatch(stopGuidedTour());\n  }, [dispatch]);"
}
```

### edit - 2026-04-08 17:22:07 UTC [19:22:07 CEST] (Redirected)

**User Request:** the new "tour" feature seems to offer "randomly related (?) nodes" - I would have expected that you take me through the nodes which are presented as related - and before the user clicks on (tour), you could fade in/out the related nodes (in the sequence if the tour) as well as the tour button to invite the user to take a tour

**Tool:** edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "filePath": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/_work/rapid-automations/integrations/operational-knowledge-<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>sal.ts",
  "oldString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a recommended reading order for nodes starting from a selected entity.\n * Two strategies:\n *   1. Incident/operational: prioritise causal chains (CAUSED_BY, HAS_ROOT_CAUSE,\n *      HAS_SYMPTOM) then resolutions, then structural, then operational edges.\n *   2. Documentation/business: follow PART_OF/CONTAINS/DERIVED_FROM hierarchy.\n *\n * The output is an ordered list of entity keys the user should visit.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    // Documentation mode: structural edges first\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  // Incident / operational mode: causal chain first\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided reading sequence from a starting entity.\n *\n * Uses priority-weighted BFS: edges with lower priority tiers are explored\n * before higher ones.  Limits the sequence to `maxNodes` to avoid\n * overwhelming the user.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n * @param maxNodes  Maximum number of nodes in the sequence (default 12).\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n  maxNodes = 12,\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [] };\n\n  // Determine mode based on the starting entity's ontology class\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Build adjacency list: key -> sorted neighbor list\n  // Each neighbor entry: { key, edgeType, priority }\n  interface Neighbor { key: string; edgeType: string; priority: number }\n  const adjacency = new Map<string, Neighbor[]>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    const addNeighbor = (from: string, to: string) => {\n      if (!entityMap.has(to)) return;\n      const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n      if (!adjacency.has(from)) adjacency.set(from, []);\n      adjacency.get(from)!.push({ key: to, edgeType: edge.type, priority: prio });\n    };\n    addNeighbor(edge.source, edge.target);\n    addNeighbor(edge.target, edge.source);\n  }\n\n  // Sort each adjacency list by priority (stable — preserves insertion order for ties)\n  for (const [, neighbors] of adjacency) {\n    neighbors.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);\n  }\n\n  // Priority BFS — process neighbors in priority order\n  const visited = new Set<string>();\n  const result: string[] = [];\n\n  // Use a simple queue seeded with the start node\n  const queue: string[] = [startKey];\n  visited.add(startKey);\n\n  while (queue.length > 0 && result.length < maxNodes) {\n    const current = queue.shift()!;\n    result.push(current);\n\n    const neighbors = adjacency.get(current) || [];\n    for (const n of neighbors) {\n      if (!visited.has(n.key) && result.length + queue.length < maxNodes) {\n        visited.add(n.key);\n        queue.push(n.key);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const labels = result.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n\n  return { nodeKeys: result, labels };\n}",
  "newString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a tour through the **direct neighbors** of the selected entity —\n * exactly the nodes shown in the Relationships panel.  The sequence starts\n * with the seed node and then visits each direct neighbor ordered by edge-type\n * priority (causal first, correlation last).\n *\n * Two priority strategies based on the starting entity's ontology class:\n *   1. Incident/operational (default): causal > resolution > structural > operational > data-flow.\n *   2. Documentation/business: structural > resolution > causal > operational > data-flow.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n  /** The edge type connecting each neighbor to the seed (index 0 is empty for seed). */\n  edgeTypes: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided tour through the direct neighbors of a starting entity.\n *\n * The result is [seed, ...directNeighbors] where neighbors are sorted by\n * edge-type priority.  This matches exactly what the user sees in the\n * Relationships section of the detail panel — no multi-hop surprises.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [], edgeTypes: [] };\n\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Collect direct neighbors with their best (lowest) edge priority.\n  // A neighbor may be connected via multiple edge types — keep the\n  // highest-priority (lowest number) one for ordering, but deduplicate\n  // the neighbor itself.\n  const neighborBest = new Map<string, { priority: number; edgeType: string }>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    let neighborKey: string | null = null;\n    if (edge.source === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.target)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.target;\n    } else if (edge.target === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.source)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.source;\n    }\n    if (!neighborKey) continue;\n\n    const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n    const existing = neighborBest.get(neighborKey);\n    if (!existing || prio < existing.priority) {\n      neighborBest.set(neighborKey, { priority: prio, edgeType: edge.type });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Sort neighbors by priority (lower = visit first), then alphabetically by name for stability\n  const sorted = [...neighborBest.entries()].sort((a, b) => {\n    const prioDiff = a[1].priority - b[1].priority;\n    if (prioDiff !== 0) return prioDiff;\n    const nameA = entityMap.get(a[0])?.name ?? a[0];\n    const nameB = entityMap.get(b[0])?.name ?? b[0];\n    return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n  });\n\n  const nodeKeys = [startKey, ...sorted.map(([k]) => k)];\n  const labels = nodeKeys.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n  const edgeTypes = ['', ...sorted.map(([, v]) => v.edgeType)];\n\n  return { nodeKeys, labels, edgeTypes };\n}"
}

Each neighbor is\n  // highlighted for 1.5s, then the next one.  This gives the user a subtle\n  // preview of what the Tour will cover and draws attention to the Tour button.\n  const previewIntervalRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null>(null);\n  const previewIndexRef = useRef(0);\n\n  const neighborKeys = useMemo(() => {\n    if (!selectedKey) return [];\n    return getDirectNeighborKeys(selectedKey, entities, edges);\n  }, [selectedKey, entities, edges]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // Clear any existing interval\n    if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n      clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n      previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n    }\n\n    // Only run preview when: node selected, tour NOT active, has neighbors\n    if (!selectedKey || guidedTourActive || neighborKeys.length === 0) {\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Start cycling after a short initial delay\n    previewIndexRef.current = 0;\n    dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[0]));\n\n    previewIntervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {\n      previewIndexRef.current = (previewIndexRef.current + 1) % neighborKeys.length;\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[previewIndexRef.current]));\n    }, 1500);\n\n    return () => {\n      if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n        clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n        previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n      }\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n    };\n  }, [selectedKey, guidedTourActive, neighborKeys, dispatch]);",

  "filePath": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/_work/rapid-automations/integrations/operational-knowledge-<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>sal.ts",
  "oldString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a recommended reading order for nodes starting from a selected entity.\n * Two strategies:\n *   1. Incident/operational: prioritise causal chains (CAUSED_BY, HAS_ROOT_CAUSE,\n *      HAS_SYMPTOM) then resolutions, then structural, then operational edges.\n *   2. Documentation/business: follow PART_OF/CONTAINS/DERIVED_FROM hierarchy.\n *\n * The output is an ordered list of entity keys the user should visit.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    // Documentation mode: structural edges first\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  // Incident / operational mode: causal chain first\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided reading sequence from a starting entity.\n *\n * Uses priority-weighted BFS: edges with lower priority tiers are explored\n * before higher ones.  Limits the sequence to `maxNodes` to avoid\n * overwhelming the user.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n * @param maxNodes  Maximum number of nodes in the sequence (default 12).\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n  maxNodes = 12,\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [] };\n\n  // Determine mode based on the starting entity's ontology class\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Build adjacency list: key -> sorted neighbor list\n  // Each neighbor entry: { key, edgeType, priority }\n  interface Neighbor { key: string; edgeType: string; priority: number }\n  const adjacency = new Map<string, Neighbor[]>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    const addNeighbor = (from: string, to: string) => {\n      if (!entityMap.has(to)) return;\n      const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n      if (!adjacency.has(from)) adjacency.set(from, []);\n      adjacency.get(from)!.push({ key: to, edgeType: edge.type, priority: prio });\n    };\n    addNeighbor(edge.source, edge.target);\n    addNeighbor(edge.target, edge.source);\n  }\n\n  // Sort each adjacency list by priority (stable — preserves insertion order for ties)\n  for (const [, neighbors] of adjacency) {\n    neighbors.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);\n  }\n\n  // Priority BFS — process neighbors in priority order\n  const visited = new Set<string>();\n  const result: string[] = [];\n\n  // Use a simple queue seeded with the start node\n  const queue: string[] = [startKey];\n  visited.add(startKey);\n\n  while (queue.length > 0 && result.length < maxNodes) {\n    const current = queue.shift()!;\n    result.push(current);\n\n    const neighbors = adjacency.get(current) || [];\n    for (const n of neighbors) {\n      if (!visited.has(n.key) && result.length + queue.length < maxNodes) {\n        visited.add(n.key);\n        queue.push(n.key);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const labels = result.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n\n  return { nodeKeys: result, labels };\n}",

The sequence starts\n * with the seed node and then visits each direct neighbor ordered by edge-type\n * priority (causal first, correlation last).\n *\n * Two priority strategies based on the starting entity's ontology class:\n *   1. Incident/operational (default): causal > resolution > structural > operational > data-flow.\n *   2. Documentation/business: structural > resolution > causal > operational > data-flow.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n  /** The edge type connecting each neighbor to the seed (index 0 is empty for seed). */\n  edgeTypes: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided tour through the direct neighbors of a starting entity.\n *\n * The result is [seed, ...directNeighbors] where neighbors are sorted by\n * edge-type priority.  This matches exactly what the user sees in the\n * Relationships section of the detail panel — no multi-hop surprises.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [], edgeTypes: [] };\n\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Collect direct neighbors with their best (lowest) edge priority.\n  // A neighbor may be connected via multiple edge types — keep the\n  // highest-priority (lowest number) one for ordering, but deduplicate\n  // the neighbor itself.\n  const neighborBest = new Map<string, { priority: number; edgeType: string }>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    let neighborKey: string | null = null;\n    if (edge.source === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.target)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.target;\n    } else if (edge.target === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.source)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.source;\n    }\n    if (!neighborKey) continue;\n\n    const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n    const existing = neighborBest.get(neighborKey);\n    if (!existing || prio < existing.priority) {\n      neighborBest.set(neighborKey, { priority: prio, edgeType: edge.type });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Sort neighbors by priority (lower = visit first), then alphabetically by name for stability\n  const sorted = [...neighborBest.entries()].sort((a, b) => {\n    const prioDiff = a[1].priority - b[1].priority;\n    if (prioDiff !== 0) return prioDiff;\n    const nameA = entityMap.get(a[0])?.name ?? a[0];\n    const nameB = entityMap.get(b[0])?.name ?? b[0];\n    return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n  });\n\n  const nodeKeys = [startKey, ...sorted.map(([k]) => k)];\n  const labels = nodeKeys.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n  const edgeTypes = ['', ...sorted.map(([, v]) => v.edgeType)];\n\n  return { nodeKeys, labels, edgeTypes };\n}"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
Edit applied successfully.

  "newString": "/**\n * Get the subset of upcoming node keys for visual hinting.\n * Returns the next N nodes after the current position (not including current).\n */\nexport function getUpcomingKeys(\n  sequence: Pick<GuidedSequence, 'nodeKeys'>,\n  currentIndex: number,\n  count = 3,\n): string[] {\n  if (sequence.nodeKeys.length === 0) return [];\n  const start = currentIndex + 1;\n  return sequence.nodeKeys.slice(start, start + count);\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute the set of direct neighbor keys for a given entity.\n * Used by the pre-tour preview animation to know which nodes to cycle through.\n */\nexport function getDirectNeighborKeys(\n  entityKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n): string[] {\n  const entitySet = new Set(entities.map((e) => e.key));\n  const neighbors = new Set<string>();\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    if (edge.source === entityKey && entitySet.has(edge.target)) {\n      neighbors.add(edge.target);\n    } else if (edge.target === entityKey && entitySet.has(edge.source)) {\n      neighbors.add(edge.source);\n    }\n  }\n  return [...neighbors];\n}"
}

Each neighbor is\n  // highlighted for 1.5s, then the next one.  This gives the user a subtle\n  // preview of what the Tour will cover and draws attention to the Tour button.\n  const previewIntervalRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null>(null);\n  const previewIndexRef = useRef(0);\n\n  const neighborKeys = useMemo(() => {\n    if (!selectedKey) return [];\n    return getDirectNeighborKeys(selectedKey, entities, edges);\n  }, [selectedKey, entities, edges]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // Clear any existing interval\n    if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n      clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n      previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n    }\n\n    // Only run preview when: node selected, tour NOT active, has neighbors\n    if (!selectedKey || guidedTourActive || neighborKeys.length === 0) {\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Start cycling after a short initial delay\n    previewIndexRef.current = 0;\n    dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[0]));\n\n    previewIntervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {\n      previewIndexRef.current = (previewIndexRef.current + 1) % neighborKeys.length;\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[previewIndexRef.current]));\n    }, 1500);\n\n    return () => {\n      if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n        clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n        previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n      }\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n    };\n  }, [selectedKey, guidedTourActive, neighborKeys, dispatch]);",

### edit - 2026-04-08 17:22:07 UTC [19:22:07 CEST] (Redirected)

**User Request:** the new "tour" feature seems to offer "randomly related (?) nodes" - I would have expected that you take me through the nodes which are presented as related - and before the user clicks on (tour), you could fade in/out the related nodes (in the sequence if the tour) as well as the tour button to invite the user to take a tour

**Tool:** edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "filePath": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/_work/rapid-automations/integrations/operational-knowledge-<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>sal.ts",
  "oldString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a recommended reading order for nodes starting from a selected entity.\n * Two strategies:\n *   1. Incident/operational: prioritise causal chains (CAUSED_BY, HAS_ROOT_CAUSE,\n *      HAS_SYMPTOM) then resolutions, then structural, then operational edges.\n *   2. Documentation/business: follow PART_OF/CONTAINS/DERIVED_FROM hierarchy.\n *\n * The output is an ordered list of entity keys the user should visit.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    // Documentation mode: structural edges first\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  // Incident / operational mode: causal chain first\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided reading sequence from a starting entity.\n *\n * Uses priority-weighted BFS: edges with lower priority tiers are explored\n * before higher ones.  Limits the sequence to `maxNodes` to avoid\n * overwhelming the user.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n * @param maxNodes  Maximum number of nodes in the sequence (default 12).\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n  maxNodes = 12,\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [] };\n\n  // Determine mode based on the starting entity's ontology class\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Build adjacency list: key -> sorted neighbor list\n  // Each neighbor entry: { key, edgeType, priority }\n  interface Neighbor { key: string; edgeType: string; priority: number }\n  const adjacency = new Map<string, Neighbor[]>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    const addNeighbor = (from: string, to: string) => {\n      if (!entityMap.has(to)) return;\n      const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n      if (!adjacency.has(from)) adjacency.set(from, []);\n      adjacency.get(from)!.push({ key: to, edgeType: edge.type, priority: prio });\n    };\n    addNeighbor(edge.source, edge.target);\n    addNeighbor(edge.target, edge.source);\n  }\n\n  // Sort each adjacency list by priority (stable — preserves insertion order for ties)\n  for (const [, neighbors] of adjacency) {\n    neighbors.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);\n  }\n\n  // Priority BFS — process neighbors in priority order\n  const visited = new Set<string>();\n  const result: string[] = [];\n\n  // Use a simple queue seeded with the start node\n  const queue: string[] = [startKey];\n  visited.add(startKey);\n\n  while (queue.length > 0 && result.length < maxNodes) {\n    const current = queue.shift()!;\n    result.push(current);\n\n    const neighbors = adjacency.get(current) || [];\n    for (const n of neighbors) {\n      if (!visited.has(n.key) && result.length + queue.length < maxNodes) {\n        visited.add(n.key);\n        queue.push(n.key);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const labels = result.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n\n  return { nodeKeys: result, labels };\n}",
  "newString": "/**\n * Guided Traversal — Reading Sequence Computation\n *\n * Computes a tour through the **direct neighbors** of the selected entity —\n * exactly the nodes shown in the Relationships panel.  The sequence starts\n * with the seed node and then visits each direct neighbor ordered by edge-type\n * priority (causal first, correlation last).\n *\n * Two priority strategies based on the starting entity's ontology class:\n *   1. Incident/operational (default): causal > resolution > structural > operational > data-flow.\n *   2. Documentation/business: structural > resolution > causal > operational > data-flow.\n */\n\nimport type { ViewerEntity, ViewerEdge } from '../api/okbClient';\n\n// --- Edge priority tiers (lower = visit sooner) ---\n\nconst CAUSAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'CAUSED_BY', 'CAUSED', 'HAS_ROOT_CAUSE', 'HAS_SYMPTOM', 'INDICATES',\n]);\n\nconst RESOLUTION_EDGES = new Set([\n  'RESOLVES', 'MITIGATES', 'APPLIED_TO', 'APPLIES_TO', 'MATCHES',\n]);\n\nconst STRUCTURAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'DERIVED_FROM', 'PART_OF', 'CONTAINS', 'HAS_TYPE', 'HAS_VERSION',\n]);\n\nconst OPERATIONAL_EDGES = new Set([\n  'OBSERVED_IN', 'LOCATED_IN', 'DEPLOYED_ON', 'RUNS_ON', 'RUNS_IN', 'MANAGED_BY',\n]);\n\nconst DATA_FLOW_EDGES = new Set([\n  'READS', 'PROCESSES', 'CONSUMED_BY', 'STORED_IN', 'USES',\n]);\n\nconst BUSINESS_CLASSES = new Set([\n  'Decision', 'Requirement', 'Risk', 'ActionItem', 'DocumentSource',\n]);\n\n/** Assign a priority tier to an edge type (lower = higher priority). */\nfunction edgePriority(edgeType: string, isDocMode: boolean): number {\n  if (isDocMode) {\n    if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n    if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n    if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n    if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n    if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n    if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n    return 5;\n  }\n  if (CAUSAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 0;\n  if (RESOLUTION_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 1;\n  if (STRUCTURAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 2;\n  if (OPERATIONAL_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 3;\n  if (DATA_FLOW_EDGES.has(edgeType)) return 4;\n  if (edgeType === 'CORRELATED_WITH') return 6;\n  return 5;\n}\n\nexport interface GuidedSequence {\n  /** Ordered list of entity keys to visit (starts with the seed node). */\n  nodeKeys: string[];\n  /** Human-readable label for each step (entity name). */\n  labels: string[];\n  /** The edge type connecting each neighbor to the seed (index 0 is empty for seed). */\n  edgeTypes: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute a guided tour through the direct neighbors of a starting entity.\n *\n * The result is [seed, ...directNeighbors] where neighbors are sorted by\n * edge-type priority.  This matches exactly what the user sees in the\n * Relationships section of the detail panel — no multi-hop surprises.\n *\n * @param startKey  Key of the entity where the user is currently focused.\n * @param entities  All visible entities.\n * @param edges     All visible edges.\n */\nexport function computeGuidedSequence(\n  startKey: string,\n  entities: ViewerEntity[],\n  edges: ViewerEdge[],\n): GuidedSequence {\n  const entityMap = new Map<string, ViewerEntity>();\n  for (const e of entities) entityMap.set(e.key, e);\n\n  const startEntity = entityMap.get(startKey);\n  if (!startEntity) return { nodeKeys: [], labels: [], edgeTypes: [] };\n\n  const isDocMode = !!(startEntity.ontologyClass && BUSINESS_CLASSES.has(startEntity.ontologyClass));\n\n  // Collect direct neighbors with their best (lowest) edge priority.\n  // A neighbor may be connected via multiple edge types — keep the\n  // highest-priority (lowest number) one for ordering, but deduplicate\n  // the neighbor itself.\n  const neighborBest = new Map<string, { priority: number; edgeType: string }>();\n\n  for (const edge of edges) {\n    let neighborKey: string | null = null;\n    if (edge.source === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.target)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.target;\n    } else if (edge.target === startKey && entityMap.has(edge.source)) {\n      neighborKey = edge.source;\n    }\n    if (!neighborKey) continue;\n\n    const prio = edgePriority(edge.type, isDocMode);\n    const existing = neighborBest.get(neighborKey);\n    if (!existing || prio < existing.priority) {\n      neighborBest.set(neighborKey, { priority: prio, edgeType: edge.type });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Sort neighbors by priority (lower = visit first), then alphabetically by name for stability\n  const sorted = [...neighborBest.entries()].sort((a, b) => {\n    const prioDiff = a[1].priority - b[1].priority;\n    if (prioDiff !== 0) return prioDiff;\n    const nameA = entityMap.get(a[0])?.name ?? a[0];\n    const nameB = entityMap.get(b[0])?.name ?? b[0];\n    return nameA.localeCompare(nameB);\n  });\n\n  const nodeKeys = [startKey, ...sorted.map(([k]) => k)];\n  const labels = nodeKeys.map((key) => entityMap.get(key)?.name ?? key);\n  const edgeTypes = ['', ...sorted.map(([, v]) => v.edgeType)];\n\n  return { nodeKeys, labels, edgeTypes };\n}"
}

Each neighbor is\n  // highlighted for 1.5s, then the next one.  This gives the user a subtle\n  // preview of what the Tour will cover and draws attention to the Tour button.\n  const previewIntervalRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null>(null);\n  const previewIndexRef = useRef(0);\n\n  const neighborKeys = useMemo(() => {\n    if (!selectedKey) return [];\n    return getDirectNeighborKeys(selectedKey, entities, edges);\n  }, [selectedKey, entities, edges]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // Clear any existing interval\n    if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n      clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n      previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n    }\n\n    // Only run preview when: node selected, tour NOT active, has neighbors\n    if (!selectedKey || guidedTourActive || neighborKeys.length === 0) {\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Start cycling after a short initial delay\n    previewIndexRef.current = 0;\n    dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[0]));\n\n    previewIntervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {\n      previewIndexRef.current = (previewIndexRef.current + 1) % neighborKeys.length;\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(neighborKeys[previewIndexRef.current]));\n    }, 1500);\n\n    return () => {\n      if (previewIntervalRef.current) {\n        clearInterval(previewIntervalRef.current);\n        previewIntervalRef.current = null;\n      }\n      dispatch(setTourPreviewKey(null));\n    };\n  }, [selectedKey, guidedTourActive, neighborKeys, dispatch]);",
